  <a id="22008" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="22016" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#22016" class="Function">σ</a> <a id="22018" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22020" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="22022" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22023" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#22023" class="Bound">A</a><a id="22024" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22026" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="22028" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#21962" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="22030" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#8917" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="22032" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#21970" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="22034" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#9823" class="Datatype Operator">∋</a> <a id="22036" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#22023" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="22038" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="22040" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#21962" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="22042" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#11094" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="22044" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#22023" class="Bound">A</a>
  <a id="22048" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#22016" class="Function">σ</a> <a id="22050" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#9859" class="InductiveConstructor">Z</a>      <a id="22057" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="22060" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#21975" class="Bound">M</a>
  <a id="22064" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#22016" class="Function">σ</a> <a id="22066" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22067" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#9906" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">S</a> <a id="22069" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#22069" class="Bound">x</a><a id="22070" class="Symbol">)</a>  <a id="22073" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="22076" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#11130" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="22078" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#22069" class="Bound">x</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}In a term of type `A` over context `Γ , B`, we replace the
variable of type `B` by a term of type `B` over context `Γ`.
To do so, we use a map from the context `Γ , B` to the context
`Γ`, that maps the last variable in the context to the term of
type `B` and every other free variable to itself.

Consider the previous example:

* `` (ƛ "z" ⇒ ` "s" · (` "s" · ` "z")) [ "s" := sucᶜ ] `` yields
  `` ƛ "z" ⇒ sucᶜ · (sucᶜ · ` "z") ``

Here is the example formalised:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="M₂"></a><a id="22553" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#22553" class="Function">M₂</a> <a id="22556" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22558" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#8901" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a> <a id="22560" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#8917" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="22562" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#8757" class="InductiveConstructor">`ℕ</a> <a id="22565" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#8730" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="22567" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#8757" class="InductiveConstructor">`ℕ</a> <a id="22570" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#11094" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="22572" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#8757" class="InductiveConstructor">`ℕ</a> <a id="22575" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#8730" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="22577" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#8757" class="InductiveConstructor">`ℕ</a>
<a id="22580" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#22553" class="Function">M₂</a> <a id="22583" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="22585" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#11182" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="22587" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#13523" class="Function Operator">#</a> <a id="22589" class="Number">1</a> <a id="22591" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#11249" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="22593" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22594" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#13523" class="Function Operator">#</a> <a id="22596" class="Number">1</a> <a id="22598" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#11249" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="22600" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#13523" class="Function Operator">#</a> <a id="22602" class="Number">0</a><a id="22603" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="M₃"></a><a id="22606" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#22606" class="Function">M₃</a> <a id="22609" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22611" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#8901" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a> <a id="22613" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#11094" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="22615" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#8757" class="InductiveConstructor">`ℕ</a> <a id="22618" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#8730" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="22620" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#8757" class="InductiveConstructor">`ℕ</a>

<a id="22701" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#22701" class="Function">_</a> <a id="22703" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22705" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#22553" class="Function">M₂</a> <a id="22708" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#21867" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="22710" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#22606" class="Function">M₃</a> <a id="22713" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#21867" class="Function Operator">]</a> <a id="22715" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#125" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="22717" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#22640" class="Function">M₄</a>
<a id="22720" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="22722" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="22724" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#182" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
Previously, we presented an example of substitution that we
did not implement, since it needed to rename the bound
variable to avoid capture:

* `` (ƛ "x" ⇒ ` "x" · ` "y") [ "y" := ` "x" · `zero ] `` should yield
  `` ƛ "z" ⇒ ` "z" · (` "x" · `zero) ``

Say the bound `"x"` has type `` `ℕ ⇒ `ℕ ``, the substituted
`"y"` has type `` `ℕ ``, and the free `"x"` also has type ``
`ℕ ⇒ `ℕ ``.  Here is the example formalised:

<a id="23319" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#23319" class="Function">_</a> <a id="23321" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23323" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#23158" class="Function">M₅</a> <a id="23326" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#21867" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="23328" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#23215" class="Function">M₆</a> <a id="23331" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#21867" class="Function Operator">]</a> <a id="23333" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#125" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="23335" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#23255" class="Function">M₇</a>
<a id="23338" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="23340" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23342" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#182" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
The logician Haskell Curry observed that getting the
definition of substitution right can be a tricky business.  It
can be even trickier when using de Bruijn indices, which can
often be hard to decipher.  Under the current approach, any
definition of substitution must, of necessity, preserves
types.  While this makes the definition more involved, it
means that once it is done the hardest work is out of the way.
And combining definition with proof makes it harder for errors
to sneak in.


## Values

The definition of value is much as before, save that the
added types incorporate the same information found in the
Canonical Forms lemma:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="23998" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Value"></a><a id="24003" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#24003" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="24009" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24011" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="24013" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24014" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#24014" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="24016" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#24016" class="Bound">A</a><a id="24017" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24019" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24021" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#24014" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="24023" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#11094" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="24025" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#24016" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24027" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24029" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="24033" class="Keyword">where</a>

      <a id="24080" class="Comment">---------------------------</a>
    <a id="24112" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24114" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#24003" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="24120" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24121" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#11182" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="24123" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#24059" class="Bound">N</a><a id="24124" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="Value.V-zero"></a><a id="24129" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#24129" class="InductiveConstructor">V-zero</a> <a id="24136" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24138" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="24140" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24141" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#24141" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="24142" class="Symbol">}</a>
      <a id="24150" class="Comment">-----------------</a>
    <a id="24172" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24174" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#24003" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="24180" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24181" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#11324" class="InductiveConstructor">`zero</a> <a id="24187" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24188" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#24141" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="24189" class="Symbol">})</a>

  <a id="Value.V-suc"></a><a id="24195" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#24195" class="InductiveConstructor">V-suc</a> <a id="24201" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24203" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="24205" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24206" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#24206" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="24207" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24209" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24210" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#24210" class="Bound">V</a> <a id="24212" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24214" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#24206" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="24216" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#11094" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="24218" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#8757" class="InductiveConstructor">`ℕ</a><a id="24220" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="24226" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24228" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#24003" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="24234" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#24210" class="Bound">V</a>
      <a id="24242" class="Comment">--------------</a>
    <a id="24261" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24263" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#24003" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="24269" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24270" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#11370" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`suc</a> <a id="24275" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#24210" class="Bound">V</a><a id="24276" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
Here `zero` requires an implicit parameter to aid inference,
much in the same way that `[]` did in
[Lists]({{ site.baseurl }}/Lists/).


## Reduction

The reduction rules are the same as those given earlier, save
that for each term we must specify its types.  As before, we
have compatibility rules that reduce a part of a term,
labelled with `ξ`, and rules that simplify a constructor
combined with a destructor, labelled with `β`:

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="24721" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="24727" class="Number">2</a> <a id="24729" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#24740" class="Datatype Operator">_—→_</a>

      <a id="25658" class="Comment">----------------</a>
    <a id="25679" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="25681" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#11515" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">μ</a> <a id="25683" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#25637" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="25685" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#24740" class="Datatype Operator">—→</a> <a id="25688" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#25637" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="25690" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#21867" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="25692" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#11515" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">μ</a> <a id="25694" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#25637" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="25696" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#21867" class="Function Operator">]</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}The definition states that `M —→ N` can only hold of terms `M`
and `N` which _both_ have type `Γ ⊢ A` for some context `Γ`
and type `A`.  In other words, it is _built-in_ to our
definition that reduction preserves types.  There is no
separate Preservation theorem to prove.  The Agda type-checker
validates that each term preserves types.  In the case of `β`
rules, preservation depends on the fact that substitution
preserves types, which is built-in to our
definition of substitution.


## Reflexive and transitive closure

The reflexive and transitive closure is exactly as before.
We simply cut-and-paste the previous definition:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="26340" class="Keyword">infix</a>  <a id="26347" class="Number">2</a> <a id="26349" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#26405" class="Datatype Operator">_—↠_</a>
<a id="26354" class="Keyword">infix</a>  <a id="26361" class="Number">1</a> <a id="26363" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#26606" class="Function Operator">begin_</a>
<a id="26370" class="Keyword">infixr</a> <a id="26377" class="Number">2</a> <a id="26379" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#26509" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_—→⟨_⟩_</a>
<a id="26387" class="Keyword">infix</a>  <a id="26394" class="Number">3</a> <a id="26396" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#26455" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_∎</a>

<a id="26400" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="_—↠_"></a><a id="26405" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#26405" class="Datatype Operator">_—↠_</a> <a id="26410" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="26412" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="26414" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="26415" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#26415" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="26417" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#26417" class="Bound">A</a><a id="26418" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="26420" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="26422" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="26423" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#26415" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="26425" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#11094" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="26427" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#26417" class="Bound">A</a><a id="26428" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="26430" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="26432" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="26433" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#26415" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="26435" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#11094" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="26437" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#26417" class="Bound">A</a><a id="26438" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="26440" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="26442" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="26446" class="Keyword">where</a>

## Examples

We reiterate each of our previous examples.  First, the Church
numeral two applied to the successor function and zero yields
the natural number two:

</pre>{% endraw %}As before, we need to supply an explicit context to `` `zero ``.

Next, a sample reduction demonstrating that two plus two is four:

    <a id="28413" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#11370" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`suc</a> <a id="28418" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28419" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#11370" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`suc</a> <a id="28424" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28425" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#11426" class="InductiveConstructor">case</a> <a id="28430" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#11324" class="InductiveConstructor">`zero</a> <a id="28436" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28437" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#13966" class="Function">two</a><a id="28440" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28442" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28443" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#11370" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`suc</a> <a id="28448" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28449" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#14010" class="Function">plus</a> <a id="28454" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#11249" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="28456" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#11130" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="28458" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#9859" class="InductiveConstructor">Z</a> <a id="28460" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#11249" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="28462" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#13966" class="Function">two</a><a id="28465" class="Symbol">))))</a>
  <a id="28472" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#26509" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">—→⟨</a> <a id="28476" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#25137" class="InductiveConstructor">ξ-suc</a> <a id="28482" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28483" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#25137" class="InductiveConstructor">ξ-suc</a> <a id="28489" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#25375" class="InductiveConstructor">β-zero</a><a id="28495" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28497" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#26509" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
   <a id="28502" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#11370" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`suc</a> <a id="28507" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28508" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#11370" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`suc</a> <a id="28513" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28514" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#11370" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`suc</a> <a id="28519" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28520" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#11370" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`suc</a> <a id="28525" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#11324" class="InductiveConstructor">`zero</a><a id="28530" class="Symbol">)))</a>
  <a id="28536" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#26455" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∎</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
And finally, a similar sample reduction for Church numerals:

## Values do not reduce

We have now completed all the definitions, which of
necessity subsumed some of the propositions from the
earlier development: Canonical Forms,
Substitution preserves types, and Preservation.
We now turn to proving the remaining results from the
previous development.

#### Exercise `V¬—→` (practice)

Following the previous development, show values do
not reduce, and its corollary, terms that reduce are not
values.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="30188" class="Comment">-- Your code goes here</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
## Progress

As before, every term that is well typed and closed is either
a value or takes a reduction step.  The formulation of progress
is just as before, but annotated with types:

## Evaluation

Before, we combined progress and preservation to evaluate a term.
We can do much the same here, but we no longer need to explicitly
refer to preservation, since it is built-in to the definition of reduction.

As previously, gas is specified by a natural number:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="31912" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Gas"></a><a id="31917" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#31917" class="Datatype">Gas</a> <a id="31921" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31923" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="31927" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="Gas.gas"></a><a id="31935" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#31935" class="InductiveConstructor">gas</a> <a id="31939" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31941" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#165" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="31943" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="31945" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#31917" class="Datatype">Gas</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}When our evaluator returns a term `N`, it will either give evidence that
`N` is a value or indicate that it ran out of gas:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="32081" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Finished"></a><a id="32086" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#32086" class="Datatype">Finished</a> <a id="32095" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="32096" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#32096" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="32098" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#32098" class="Bound">A</a><a id="32099" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="32101" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32102" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#32102" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="32104" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="32106" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#32096" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="32108" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#11094" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="32110" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#32098" class="Bound">A</a><a id="32111" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="32113" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="32115" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="32119" class="Keyword">where</a>

   <a id="Finished.done"></a><a id="32129" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#32129" class="InductiveConstructor">done</a> <a id="32134" class="Symbol">:</a>
       <a id="32143" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#24003" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="32149" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#32102" class="Bound">N</a>
       <a id="32158" class="Comment">----------</a>
     <a id="32174" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="32176" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#32086" class="Datatype">Finished</a> <a id="32185" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#32102" class="Bound">N</a>

   <a id="Finished.out-of-gas"></a><a id="32191" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#32191" class="InductiveConstructor">out-of-gas</a> <a id="32202" class="Symbol">:</a>
       <a id="32211" class="Comment">----------</a>
       <a id="32229" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#32086" class="Datatype">Finished</a> <a id="32238" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#32102" class="Bound">N</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}Given a term `L` of type `A`, the evaluator will, for some `N`, return
a reduction sequence from `L` to `N` and an indication of whether
reduction finished:
{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="32405" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Steps"></a><a id="32410" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#32410" class="Datatype">Steps</a> <a id="32416" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="32418" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="32420" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="32421" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#32421" class="Bound">A</a><a id="32422" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="32424" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="32426" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#8901" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a> <a id="32428" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#11094" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="32430" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#32421" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="32432" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="32434" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="32438" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="Steps.steps"></a><a id="32447" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#32447" class="InductiveConstructor">steps</a> <a id="32453" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="32455" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="32457" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="32458" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#32458" class="Bound">A</a><a id="32459" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="32461" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="32462" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#32462" class="Bound">L</a> <a id="32464" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#32464" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="32466" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="32468" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#8901" class="InductiveConstructor">∅</a> <a id="32470" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#11094" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="32472" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#32458" class="Bound">A</a><a id="32473" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="32479" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="32481" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#32462" class="Bound">L</a> <a id="32483" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#26405" class="Datatype Operator">—↠</a> <a id="32486" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#32464" class="Bound">N</a>
    <a id="32492" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="32494" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#32086" class="Datatype">Finished</a> <a id="32503" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#32464" class="Bound">N</a>
      <a id="32511" class="Comment">----------</a>
    <a id="32526" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="32528" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#32410" class="Datatype">Steps</a> <a id="32534" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#32462" class="Bound">L</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}The evaluator takes gas and a term and returns the corresponding steps:

</pre>{% endraw %}The definition is a little simpler than previously, as we no longer need
to invoke preservation.

## Examples

We reiterate each of our previous examples.  We re-define the term
`sucμ` that loops forever:

<a id="37230" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="37232" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="37234" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#182" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
And the corresponding term for Church numerals:

</pre>{% endraw %}
We omit the proof that reduction is deterministic, since it is
tedious and almost identical to the previous proof.


#### Exercise `mul-example` (recommended)

Using the evaluator, confirm that two times two is four.

## Intrinsic typing is golden

Counting the lines of code is instructive.  While this chapter
covers the same formal development as the previous two
chapters, it has much less code.  Omitting all the examples,
and all proofs that appear in Properties but not DeBruijn
(such as the proof that reduction is deterministic), the
number of lines of code is as follows:

    Lambda                      216
    Properties                  235
    DeBruijn                    275

The relation between the two approaches approximates the
golden ratio: extrinsically-typed terms
require about 1.6 times as much code as intrinsicaly-typed.

## Unicode

This chapter uses the following unicode:

    σ  U+03C3  GREEK SMALL LETTER SIGMA (\Gs or \sigma)
    ₀  U+2080  SUBSCRIPT ZERO (\_0)
    ₃  U+20B3  SUBSCRIPT THREE (\_3)
    ₄  U+2084  SUBSCRIPT FOUR (\_4)
    ₅  U+2085  SUBSCRIPT FIVE (\_5)
    ₆  U+2086  SUBSCRIPT SIX (\_6)
    ₇  U+2087  SUBSCRIPT SEVEN (\_7)
    ≠  U+2260  NOT EQUAL TO (\=n)
